          <h2 class="wt-text-heading-02 wt-mb-xs-2">
           What is Etsy?
          </h2>
          <a class="wt-text-link" href="/about">
           Read our wonderfully weird story
          </a>
          <div class="wt-grid wt-pt-xs-6 wt-pl-xs-3 wt-pr-xs-3">
           <div class="wt-grid__item-md-10 wt-grid__item-offset-md-1 wt-grid__item-lg-8 wt-grid__item-offset-lg-2 wt-grid__item-offset-xl-0 wt-grid__item-xl-4 wt-mb-xs-4 wt-mb-lg-6 wt-mb-xl-2 wt-pr-sm-4 wt-pl-sm-4 wt-pr-xs-2 wt-pl-xs-2">
            <h3 class="wt-text-heading-01 wt-mb-xs-1">
             A one-of-a-kind community
            </h3>
            <p class="wt-text-body-01">
             Etsy is a global online marketplace, where people come together to make, sell, buy, and 
            collect unique items.
            </p>
           </div>
           <div class="wt-grid__item-md-10 wt-grid__item-offset-md-1 wt-grid__item-lg-8 wt-grid__item-offset-lg-2 wt-grid__item-offset-xl-0 wt-grid__item-xl-4 wt-mb-xs-4 wt-mb-lg-6 wt-mb-xl-2 wt-pr-sm-4 wt-pl-sm-4 wt-pr-xs-2 wt-pl-xs-2">
            <h3 class="wt-text-heading-01 wt-mb-xs-1">
             Support independent creators
            </h3>

  <script type="text/javascript">
   function runQualtrics() {
        try {
            if (typeof QSI !== 'undefined' && QSI.API && QSI.API.run && QSI.reg && !QSI.InterceptsRan) {
                clearInterval(window._qsiIntervalId);
                window._qsiIntervalId = null;
                QSI.API.run();
            }
        } catch (e) {
            clearInterval(window._qsiIntervalId);
            window._qsiIntervalId = null;
            if (window.Etsy && window.Etsy.Logger) {
                window.Etsy.Logger.info("Something on Qualtrics's side broke, contact #web-platform", { err: e });
            }
        }
    }
    if (window.addEventListener) {
        window.addEventListener('load', function() {
            if (typeof window._qsiIntervalId === 'undefined') {
                window._qsiIntervalId = setInterval(runQualtrics, 1000);
            }
        }, false);
    } else if (window.attachEvent) {
        window.attachEvent('onload', function() {
            if (typeof window._qsiIntervalId === 'undefined') {
                window._qsiIntervalId = setInterval(runQualtrics, 1000);
            }
        });
    }
  </script>
